    colorIdentity = "W"

    toughness = 4
    keywords(Keyword.FLYING)

package com.wingedsheep.mtg.sets.generated.demo.cards

import com.wingedsheep.sdk.scripting.references.Player
import com.wingedsheep.sdk.scripting.values.DynamicAmount


/**
 * Endless Ranks of the Dead
 * {2}{B}{B}
 * Enchantment
 * At the beginning of your upkeep, create X 2/2 black Zombie creature tokens, where X is half the number of Zombies you control, rounded down.
 */
val EndlessRanksOfTheDead = card("Endless Ranks of the Dead") {
    manaCost = "{2}{B}{B}"
    colorIdentity = "B"
    typeLine = "Enchantment"
    oracleText = "At the beginning of your upkeep, create X 2/2 black Zombie creature tokens, where X is half the number of Zombies you control, rounded down."
    triggeredAbility {
        trigger = Triggers.YourUpkeep
        effect = Effects.CreateToken(
            count = DynamicAmount.Divide(
                DynamicAmount.AggregateBattlefield(Player.You, GameObjectFilter.Creature.withSubtype("Zombie")),
                DynamicAmount.Fixed(2),
                roundUp = false
            ),
            power = 2,
            toughness = 2,
            colors = setOf(Color.BLACK),
